NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

Orient ECO Energy Limited
Registered Office: Sigappi Achi building, 4th Floor, Door No. 18/3,
Rukmani Lakshmipathi Road, (Marshalls Road), Egmore, Chennai-600 008.
(Publication in pursuance of Section 485 of the Companies Act, 1956)
Notice is hereby given in general information that the members of Orient ECO Energy Limited at its Annual General
Meeting of the Company held on Monday the 7th day of July, 2014 at its registered office have passed the following special
resolution to wind up the above Company Voluntarily:
“RESOLVED THAT Pursuant to the provisions of Section 484(1) (b) and applicable provisions, if any, of the
Companies Act, 1956 includig any statutory modification or re-enactment thereof for the time being in force, the consent of
the members of the Company be and is hereby accorded to wind up the affairs of the company as the members’
Voluntary winding up.”

Dated: 09-07-2014.
By Order of the Board.
Chennai-600 008,
18th July 2014.
VENKATACHALAM SESHA AYYAR,
Director,
Din: 06698233.
